\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{screen\_vprintf()}{screen\_vprintf()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::screen\+\_\+vprintf (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1793008155ca135d61e68f63e1a77e0f}{text\+\_\+format\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{txt\+\_\+fmt,  }\item[{const int16\+\_\+t}]{line,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{text,  }\item[{va\+\_\+list}]{args }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Print a formatted string to the screen on the specified line. 

Same as {\ttfamily display\+\_\+printf} except that this uses a {\ttfamily va\+\_\+list} instead of the ellipsis operator so this can be used by other functions.

Will default to a medium sized font by default if invalid txt\+\_\+fmt is given. Exposed mostly for writing libraries and custom functions.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+A\+C\+C\+E\+SS -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the screen mutex.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em txt\+\_\+fmt} & Text format enum that determines if the text is medium, large, medium\+\_\+center, or large\+\_\+center. (D\+O\+ES N\+OT S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT S\+M\+A\+LL) \\
\hline
{\em line} & The line number on which to print \\
\hline
{\em text} & Format string \\
\hline
{\em args} & List of arguments for the format string\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if there were no errors, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if an error occured while taking or returning the screen mutex. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_aff632a5957fe84aaff544ed4d194ccd9}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_aff632a5957fe84aaff544ed4d194ccd9}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!screen\_vprintf\_at@{screen\_vprintf\_at}}
\index{screen\_vprintf\_at@{screen\_vprintf\_at}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{screen\_vprintf\_at()}{screen\_vprintf\_at()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::screen\+\_\+vprintf\+\_\+at (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1793008155ca135d61e68f63e1a77e0f}{text\+\_\+format\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{txt\+\_\+fmt,  }\item[{const int16\+\_\+t}]{x,  }\item[{const int16\+\_\+t}]{y,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{text,  }\item[{va\+\_\+list}]{args }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Print a formatted string to the screen at the specified coordinates. 

Same as {\ttfamily display\+\_\+printf\+\_\+at} except that this uses a {\ttfamily va\+\_\+list} instead of the ellipsis operator so this can be used by other functions.

Will default to a medium sized font by default if invalid txt\+\_\+fmt is given.

Text formats medium\+\_\+center and large\+\_\+center will default to medium and large respectively. Exposed mostly for writing libraries and custom functions.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+A\+C\+C\+E\+SS -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the screen mutex.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em txt\+\_\+fmt} & Text format enum that determines if the text is small, medium, or large. \\
\hline
{\em x,y} & The (x,y) coordinates of the top left corner of the string \\
\hline
{\em text} & Format string \\
\hline
{\em args} & List of arguments for the format string\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily screen\+\_\+touch\+\_\+status\+\_\+s\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::screen\+\_\+touch\+\_\+status (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Screen Touch Functions ~\newline
 

These functions allow programmers to access ~\newline
 information about screen touches ~\newline
 Gets the touch status of the last touch of the screen.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The last\+\_\+touch\+\_\+e\+\_\+t enum specifier that indicates the last touch status of the screen (E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+L\+E\+A\+SE, E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+SS, or E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+V\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+S\+S\+\_\+\+A\+N\+D\+\_\+\+H\+O\+LD). This will be released by default if no action was taken. If an error occured, the screen\+\_\+touch\+\_\+status\+\_\+s\+\_\+t will have its last\+\_\+touch\+\_\+e\+\_\+t enum specifier set to E\+\_\+\+T\+O\+U\+C\+H\+\_\+\+E\+RR, and other values set to -\/1. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a001f29d360d7be749ff683853de89808}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a001f29d360d7be749ff683853de89808}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Serial}{Serial}} communication functions ~\newline
 

These functions allow programmers to communicate using U\+A\+RT over R\+S485 ~\newline
 Enables generic serial on the given port.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function must be called before any of the generic serial functions will work.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the port.

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!serial\_flush@{serial\_flush}}
\index{serial\_flush@{serial\_flush}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{serial\_flush()}{serial\_flush()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::serial\+\_\+flush (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Clears the internal input and output F\+I\+FO buffers. 

This can be useful to reset state and remove old, potentially unneeded data from the input F\+I\+FO buffer or to cancel sending any data in the output F\+I\+FO buffer.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function does not cause the data in the output buffer to be written, it simply clears the internal buffers. Unlike stdout, generic serial does not use buffered IO (the F\+I\+FO buffers are written as soon as possible).
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a44e637ac10841488b1e2a692cb20e733}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a44e637ac10841488b1e2a692cb20e733}}

Gets the nth largest object according to size\+\_\+id. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor E\+D\+OM -\/ size\+\_\+id is greater than the number of available objects. E\+H\+O\+S\+T\+D\+O\+WN -\/ Reading the vision sensor failed for an unknown reason.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em size\+\_\+id} & The object to read from a list roughly ordered by object size (0 is the largest item, 1 is the second largest, etc.)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t object corresponding to the given size id, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ae53aedc2122f3b4c53d5874fde408a76}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ae53aedc2122f3b4c53d5874fde408a76}}

Gets the nth largest object of the given signature according to size\+\_\+id. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ sig\+\_\+id is outside the range \mbox{[}1-\/8\mbox{]} E\+D\+OM -\/ size\+\_\+id is greater than the number of available objects. E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ Reading the vision sensor failed for an unknown reason.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em size\+\_\+id} & The object to read from a list roughly ordered by object size (0 is the largest item, 1 is the second largest, etc.) \\
\hline
{\em signature} & The signature ID \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} for which an object will be returned.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t object corresponding to the given signature and size\+\_\+id, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vision\_read\_by\_size()}{vision\_read\_by\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::vision\+\_\+read\+\_\+by\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{size\+\_\+id,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{object\+\_\+count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_ae619120558539c13e53b5a6f42fb4375}{vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{object\+\_\+arr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Reads up to object\+\_\+count object descriptors into object\+\_\+arr. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21), or fewer than object\+\_\+count number of objects were found. E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor E\+D\+OM -\/ size\+\_\+id is greater than the number of available objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
 & {\em size\+\_\+id} & The object to read from a list roughly ordered by object size (0 is the largest item, 1 is the second largest, etc.) \\
\hline
 & {\em object\+\_\+count} & The number of objects to read \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em object\+\_\+arr} & A pointer to copy the objects into\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of object signatures copied. This number will be less than object\+\_\+count if there are fewer objects detected by the vision sensor. Returns P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the port was invalid, an error occurred, or fewer objects than size\+\_\+id were found. All objects in object\+\_\+arr that were not found are given V\+I\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+IG as their signature. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a0f38715b935eae0421d59e5102d98155}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a0f38715b935eae0421d59e5102d98155}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::vision\+\_\+set\+\_\+zero\+\_\+point (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{vision\+\_\+zero\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}]{zero\+\_\+point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the (0,0) coordinate for the Field of View. 

This will affect the coordinates returned for each request for a vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t from the sensor, so it is recommended that this function only be used to configure the sensor at the beginning of its use.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em zero\+\_\+point} & One of vision\+\_\+zero\+\_\+e\+\_\+t to set the (0,0) coordinate for the F\+OV\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
